Units that march off their own works lose the cover while the visible works fade. Abatis built by a brigade in its own parapet/redoubt is marked prepared, starts stronger, slows more, bites morale/disorder/fatigue harder, clears slower, and renders with clearer stakes/backing. 2D and 3D draw hasty/parapet/redoubt shapes; the HUD names the stage and front-cover multiplier; the end card teaches the Hess/Mahan fortification lesson.

AI inline charges stay unchanged. `src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js` now wires D141 terrain through `fldCoverAt`/`fldMoveFactor`: fort strong cover + attacker friction, town hard cover + street friction, swamp soft concealment + major slow, with the old wall/woods/hill ladder retained. This is ONE universal combat model; no scenario outcome gate.

## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-26 **PHASE H В· H5 increment 3 вҖ” TERRAIN READABILITY: the modern (non-hex) engine now makes high/low ground вҖ” and EVERY topography type вҖ” EXPLICIT (D141), the THIRD step of the locked D138 arc.** Three player-chosen **elevation modes** (default **HILLSHADE** relief = T21's, no double-count В· **CONTOURS** = iso-lines + elevation labels В· **COLOR-BY-HEIGHT** = a CVD-safe **Viridis** hypsometric tint), cycled from the in-battle settings drawer + the **R** key + the legend's mode chip; an **always-on compact LEGEND** (mode chip В· viridis gradient В· a live **on-hover elevation+type readout** В· a topography key of the types present); the 2D top-down finally shows relief it never had; and **swamp / town / fort** are now distinct render types. All PRESENTATION-ONLY вҶ’ byte-identical. The hex engine IS Classic вҖ” untouched.

> **вӯҗ THE i3 DISCIPLINE (read first вҖ” the SAME as i2, NOT the i1 carve-out).** PRESENTATION-ONLY, held to the FULL D74 byte-identity law. The elevation mode is a sim-UNREAD `G.settings.fldElevMode` (the renderRich pattern вҖ” kept in `G.settings` only, NOT localStorage, so the documented "hillshade" DEFAULT holds every fresh session). The new **swamp/town/fort** terrain arrays (`__FIELD.terrain.swamps/towns/forts[]`) are **combat-INERT вҖ” read by NO sim/combat function** (a probe static-scan enforces it), so combat stays byte-identical even though terrain was ADDED вҶ’ proven `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff + `probe-bullrun` 15/15.
>
> **WHAT SHIPPED (D141) вҖ” T22 (вүҲ630 lines) + thin T0/T6 seams.** (1) **3 modes**: HILLSHADE (3D = T21's slope-AO relief, T22 adds NOTHING to the 3D ground here so relief is never double-counted; 2D paints its own cached hillshade вҖ” the top-down had none); CONTOURS (a 3D `LineSegments` of marching-squares iso-lines + elevation-label sprites; 2D = offscreen-cached polylines); COLOR-BY-HEIGHT (a 3D viridis-tinted overlay mesh; 2D = cached viridis canvas). The 3D hypso+contour are PREBUILT once and `.visible`-toggled per mode (snappy, no rebuild, no camera jerk). (2) **Legend + hover** вҖ” `#fldElevLegend` (mode chip В· viridis gradient bar В· `#fldElevHover` live readout В· topography key). (3) **swamp/town/fort** distinct in 2D + 3D (swamp = wet-teal disc + reeds; town = clustered buildings; fort = angular earthwork berm + bastions); a demo set in the sandbox showcase. T0 seams: `fldBuildTerrain` gains the demo arrays; `fld2dDraw` calls the guarded `fldTrDrawGround2d` after the field fill; `fldKey` gains the `R` branch. T6: the drawer gains an "Elevation display" cycle control.
>

> **вӯҗ THE i2 DISCIPLINE (read first вҖ” the INVERSE of i1).** i1 was the deliberate D74 byte-identity CARVE-OUT (gameplay). **i2 is the opposite: PRESENTATION-ONLY, held to the FULL D74 byte-identity law.** NEW `src/tactical/T21-visual-fidelity.js` wraps the render seams BY ASSIGNMENT (the T16/T17/T18 pattern, OUTERMOST), writes vertex COLOUR only (never a position/sim field/`fldRng`/`_SAVE_VER`), and the headless AI-vs-AI stepper never enters a 3D seam вҶ’ the per-battle outcomes stay **byte-identical: `probe-presets` 26/26 + `probe-phased-ab` 20/0-diff (final build)**.
>
> **WHY ADDITIVE, NOT A TONE-MAP FLIP (the r128 decision):** THREE is r128 (0.128.0), PRE the r152 colour-management overhaul. A grounded 5-agent recon proved a global ACES/sRGB flip would SPLIT the pipeline (the T16 smoke + T17 precip raw-`gl_FragColor` ShaderMaterials don't tone-map вҶ’ smoke darkens / rain warms, a visible seam) + force re-tuning every hardcoded colour across T0/T10/T17/T18 вҶ’ EXCLUDED. Real shadow maps (r128 InstancedMesh depth-pass blob + UHD-617 cost) + MeshStandard terrain (renders DARKER without an envMap under the linear pipeline) also excluded. The win is purely ADDITIVE + palette-preserving.
>

> **H1b deepens the flags layer that already existed (`src/tactical/T10-flags.js`; the D91 deepen-not-replace ethic) вҖ” and fixes three real defects found on recon:** the 2D path drew blank colour rectangles (it built an SVG + an `Image()` it never drew); corps-badge SHAPES were never rendered (only a text label, with a wrong map вҖ” II Corps a circle, V and VI both a generic "cross"); and badges showed on every battle regardless of date (an anachronism on the 1861-62 fields), with a roman-numeral substring bug mis-reading "II Corps" as "I Corps".
>
> **What shipped:** (1) **battle-AWARE flag selection** (`_FLD_BATTLE_META`) вҖ” **First National "Stars and Bars"** at First Bull Run (the ANV battle flag did NOT exist on 21 Jul 1861 вҖ” the smoke-confusion of the Stars and Bars with the U.S. flag THAT day is what prompted it) and in the early West (Shiloh); the **ANV battle flag (Southern Cross)** mid-war East; the **Hardee pattern** (blue + white disc) for the native Army of Tennessee; with **Longstreet's transferred Eastern brigades (Hood/Kershaw/Law) flying the ANV flag even at Chickamauga**; (2) **new patterns drawn for real** вҖ” first-national, hardee, polk (upright St-George cross, distinct from the ANV diagonal saltire), US cavalry guidon; (3) **corrected Kearny-patch corps-badge SHAPES as glyphs** вҖ” I=disc, II=trefoil, III=diamond, V=Maltese (a flared cross pattГ©e), VI=Greek cross (distinct from V), XI=crescent, XII=star вҖ” division-coloured (1st=red/2nd=white/3rd=blue), with a light parchment **halo** so the shape silhouette reads on any background, and ALWAYS paired with a text label (CVD-safe: shape + label, never colour alone); (4) the **anachronism GATE** вҖ” corps badges (Hooker's Circular, 21 Mar 1863) appear ONLY at the Eastern post-Mar-1863 fields (Chancellorsville + Gettysburg) and NEVER on Bull Run / Malvern Hill / Antietam / Fredericksburg (where the corps existed but wore no badge yet вҖ” the HUD names the adoption date there as a teaching beat); (5) a **working 2D draw** (cached canvas blit, fog-gated) + a deepened **HUD** (flag thumbnail + badge swatch + a citation-grade provenance caption).

## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-25 **PHASE H ("make it come to life") В· H4 вҖ” BATTLE-AMBIENCE AUDIO DEEPENING: a default-OFF, opt-in, stereo-spatialized procedural battle-soundscape bed вҖ” the "one continuous roar" of massed musketry, the ground-shaking bass of a cannonade, and the firing brigades' reports placed in the stereo field where the smoke actually rises вҖ” layered UNDER the existing T9 din+SFX, fog-gated so it never betrays a hidden foe. NEXT in H = H1b flags/insignia polish** (overnight run, D130)

> **H4 ships the audio "come-to-life" increment вҖ” and gives the battlefield its voice.** New `src/tactical/T19-battle-ambience.js`: a spatialized procedural bed UNDER T9's din+SFX that pairs 1:1 with the T16 gunsmoke (sound comes from where the smoke is) вҖ” (1) a continuous **rolling-fire wash** (looping band-passed noise + a slow swell-LFO, gain tracking battle intensity), (2) a **cannonade sub-bass rumble** (gated up by the count of brigades actually working their guns), (3) **located cannon/musket reports** (cannon = crack + body + rolling tail; musket = a volley "rip") panned in stereo by the firing brigade's field-x and **fog-gated** (a hidden foe makes no located sound). DEFAULT OFF; discoverable via a new accessible "Battle ambience" row on T9's audio panel; one-time captioned.

OWNS a separate AudioContext (the AUDIO_SCORE one-context-per-subsystem convention). Reads firing state READ-ONLY (`u._artFlash`/`u.targetId`/`u.ammo`/`u.state`/`u.x`/`u.id`/`u.side`/`u.alive`, `__FIELD.phase/fog/units`); writes NO sim field, NEVER `fldRng`, no `_SAVE_VER` (the `battleAmbience` flag is lazy-defaulted). Reports defer until the AudioContext is running (no first-gesture stampede); the bed self-silences on the 'over' screen (no idle-graph drain); source-voice pool bounded + all nodes disposed + the context suspended on `fldExit`. ## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-24 **PHASE H ("make it come to life") В· H3-i3 вҖ” TERRAIN & UNIT RENDER RICHNESS: the battlefield itself made to feel alive вҖ” procedural ground texture (grass / dry-ochre / mud / tilled-furrow patches), woods that sway in the wind, banner cloth that ripples, marching columns that bob, selected brigades that pulse, and a fallen brigade that fades into the ground instead of snapping out; 2D + 3D. NEXT in H = H4 audio deepening** (overnight run, D129)

> **H3-i3 ships the next "come-to-life" increment вҖ” the field, the woods, and the men all gain texture + motion.** New `src/tactical/T18-render-richness.js`: (1) **3D ground vertex-colour enrichment** вҖ” procedural grass mottle + dry-ochre / damp-lush / bare-earth patches + tilled crop-row corduroy (VERTICES recoloured only, never positions вҶ’ units still seat on the analytic `fldTerrainH`, never float/sink); (2) **woods wind-sway** (per-cone tilt-about-base on the woods `InstancedMesh`); (3) **banner cloth ripple** (per-unit flag twist/dip, whichever "flag" mesh is present вҖ” base or the T10 textured flag); (4) **selection-ring pulse** + a **march bob** for actively-moving brigades; (5) a **casualty fade-out** on death (the brigade settles toward the ground + fades over ~0.85s). Plus 2D-canvas equivalents: a CACHED soft field-grain (dry/lush/earth patches), a pulsing selection halo, the same casualty fade.
>
> **ARCHITECTURE вҖ” combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. All variation is **analytic value-noise + wall-clock sines вҖ” NEVER `fldRng`**; reads ONLY render state + read-only sim fields (`u.x`/`u.z`/`u.alive`/`u.state`/`u.id`, `__FIELD.sel`); writes NO sim field, no `_SAVE_VER`. Woods sway recomputes each instance matrix from a cached base (no drift); `fldLow()` trims sway amplitude + grain cell size; the **2D field-grain is cached to an offscreen canvas** (built once per field/scale, blitted with ONE `drawImage` вҖ” no per-frame fillrate on the weakest 2D-fallback GPU). CVD-safe (no colour-encoded info); no new DOM/text вҶ’ `wcag-auditor` N/A by construction.

Pure visual вҖ” no sim write, D74 intact. **(LOW fixes)** a **fog-ghost guard** (`rec.wasVis` вҖ” a fog-hidden enemy that dies no longer pops into view as a fading block); the **selection ring now fades with the corpse**; `_rrSetGroupOpacity` no longer flips the T10 flag's `transparent` flag (alpha-corruption fix); the **2D grain offscreen cache** (perf); `renderRich="off"` **mid-battle motion revert**; the probe **sim-field-invariance** snapshot; a counted + once-warned **`FLDRR_S.errN`** the probe asserts is 0. ## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-24 **PHASE H ("make it come to life") В· H3-i2 вҖ” WEATHER + TIME-OF-DAY ATMOSPHERE: procedural sky/light re-tint (background В· fog В· sun В· hemisphere) + rain/snow precipitation per a citation-grade per-battle `weather` hint; 2D + 3D. The marquee visible win is Antietam's dawn Cornfield ground-fog. NEXT in H3 = i3 terrain/unit render richness** (overnight run, D128)

> **H3-i2 ships the next "come-to-life" increment вҖ” and gives every battle a sky matched to its history.** New `src/tactical/T17-weather.js` re-tints the 3D `scene.background`/`fog`/sun/hemisphere AND washes the 2D canvas to a resolved `{sky, time}` palette (sky вҲҲ clear/overcast/rain/fog/haze/snow; time вҲҲ dawn/morning/midday/afternoon/dusk), plus a procedural rain/snow `THREE.Points` cloud (the T16 shader pattern) + a 2D precip hatch, and a one-time accessible weather note via the existing role=status `fldScenarioBanner`. **The marquee: Antietam's pale warm dawn Cornfield ground-fog** (distant brigades fading into the mist, the objective still readable) вҖ” the one genuinely non-clear sky; the rest carry faithful time-of-day light (warm afternoons, cool mornings).
>
> **CITATION-GRADE DATA (research+verify Workflow, 18 agents).** The verifiers REFUSED to fabricate drama вҖ” Gettysburg `hazeвҶ’clear` (Rev. Jacobs' instrument log: bright at the 2pm Pickett's-Charge window), Fredericksburg `fogвҶ’clear/afternoon` (the Rappahannock fog lifted ~10am, before the noon-to-dark assault вҖ” the note still teaches it), Shiloh `clear/morning` (the rain was OVERNIGHT), a misattributed Vicksburg source removed. **The honest finding: the "fog of war" at most of these battles was POWDER-SMOKE (already shipped via T16), not weather** вҖ” only Antietam's dawn fog is a real non-clear sky. Final hints (in `data/*.json`): bullrun1 clear/afternoon В· malvernHill clear/afternoon В· **antietam fog/dawn** В· fredericksburg clear/afternoon В· chancellorsville clear/morning В· gettysburg clear/afternoon В· shiloh clear/morning В· vicksburg clear/midday(no-op) В· chickamauga clear/afternoon.
>
> **ARCHITECTURE вҖ” combat byte-identical BY CONSTRUCTION (D74):** touches NO combat file. WRAPS `fld3dInit`/`fld3dRender`/`fld2dDraw`/`fldExit` by ASSIGNMENT (the T9/T16 seam; propagates T16's `._atmo` marker so the chain stays introspectable). Reads ONLY the scenario's `weather` hint (`_scenTop.weather` multi-phase, else `scenData.weather`) + render state; OWN LCG вҖ” **never `fldRng`** (sim seed probe-proven unchanged across the wx render loop); no sim write, no `_SAVE_VER`. **THE BYTE-IDENTICAL DEFAULT: a missing hint вҖ” or `clear`/`midday` вҖ” resolves to `null` and applies ZERO change** (every shipped look preserved). Diff = `src/tactical/T17-weather.js` (new) + `src/00-manifest.json` (T17 after T16) + 9 `data/*.json` weather blocks + `tools/probe-weather.mjs` (new) + the generated HTML.
>
> **ACCESSIBILITY / PERF (Intel UHD-617 floor):** the static tint is motion-free вҶ’ applies under `reduceMotion`; only PRECIPITATION (motion) is suppressed under it (probe-verified: tint kept, no `wxPrecip`); `G.settings.weather==="off"` disables the whole layer. Fog far-plane held **вүҘ1500** in every palette so the objective never vanishes. One precip draw call + `fldLow()` budget (520/200) + a `gl_PointSize` driver clamp. CVD-safe; no new DOM/text (the note reuses the AA-vetted banner) вҶ’ `wcag-auditor` N/A.

> **Bug-hunt (6 diverse-lens Opus finders Г— 3-skeptic default-refute + a critic; the critic leg STALLED вҶ’ substituted by an inline completeness pass, the D124 precedent) вҶ’ 1 HIGH + 1 LOW fixed:** **(HIGH)** the atmosphere note re-fired EVERY frame вҖ” `_wxLaunchKey` keyed on `__FIELD.seed` (which `fldRng` mutates each tick) вҶ’ re-keyed on the stable `__FIELD.scenario` + a note-once probe lock; **(LOW, real)** inherited-property sky names (`constructor`/`__proto__`) bypassed the `!FLDWX.SKY[sky]` guard вҶ’ `hasOwnProperty` validation + a malformed-input lock. ## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-23 **В§12.3 THE ELECTION-SUPPORT RELIEF-BIND: a commissioned UNION political general (Banks/Butler/Sigel/McClernand) costs extra political capital to relieve before the 1864 vote вҖ” the bind Lincoln lived вҖ” relaxing once the verdict is in** (overnight run, D113)

> **The GM В§12.3 command-politics keystone ships** (the bind the Commission move D109 was built around, now unblocked by the 1864-election state E4/D112). A commissioned POLITICAL general delivers his constituency's votes while he serves, so relieving him before the 1864 election forfeits that support: an ADDITIVE surcharge on his relief cost (`_cmdReliefCost`) that rises year over year toward the vote (1862<1863<1864) and FALLS to zero the moment `clock.resolved1864` is set. `surcharge = round((politicalValue/100)В·windowByYear[year]В·surchargeMax=14)`, bounded. A teaching tell on the active-general card names the constituency + the `+N capital` cost. Teaches В§12.3 concretely: a fielded Banks both fields a low commandLeadership (49 vs Grant 87, D109) AND can't be cheaply dumped before November 1864. **Picked for an autonomous tick** over the frozen-loop E4-i2 (contained command-economy, no frozen-loop, no design fork); Aaron then reordered the queue вҖ” **E1 hinge-forks next, fantastical tier first.**

## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-23 **Q12: THE DIVISION SUB-TIER вҖ” seat your generals into the DIVISION billets nested under each corps; a corps is only as good as its divisions** (overnight run, D110 вҖ” Codex code + Claude vetting/doc close-out)

> **The GM depth-chart's next rung is shipped** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.1 вҖ” Army вҶ’ Corps вҶ’ **DIVISION** вҶ’ Brigade), built on the Q10 corps chart (D108). Beyond seating IвҖ“IV Corps, the President now SEATS pool generals into each seated corps's **3 DIVISION billets**, spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the existing GM currency). A division can be staffed ONLY under a SEATED corps (the real chain of command), so the depth chart is a TREE built top-down. Teaches that a corps was only as good as its divisions вҖ” A. P. Hill's "Light Division" and Hood's/Pickett's divisions were the cutting edge of Lee's corps, **as were the Union's hard-fighting divisions in Hancock's II Corps**.

> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (byte-identical until you seat a division; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated division commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership` вҖ” an INPUT the bridge already reads вҖ” via `_cmdDivLift` = clamp(ОЈ(`effDivRating`вҲ’64)Г—0.03, Вұ2). `effDivRating` = the general's GM OVR (carries the Q9 promotion) minus a `belowGradePenalty` (4) when his grade is below the **preferredGrade** вҖ” a division was a **Maj. Gen.'s** billet in BOTH armies (distinct from the corps tier where a CS corps was a Lt. Gen.'s), so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads stretched until promoted. The lift is deliberately SMALLER than the corps lift (cap 2 vs 4) so the hierarchy holds: **army Вұ17 > corps Вұ4 > divisions Вұ2.** No division seated вҶ’ ОЈ over zero slots вҶ’ lift 0 вҶ’ the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `7d86fcf`. **ONE BILLET PER MAN** (army/corps/division mutually exclusive; seating-higher clears the division); **vacating a corps CASCADES** (orphaned divisions stop contributing lift вҖ” enforced at the READ layer `cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift`, cleaned on load-sanitize). `cmd.divisions = {corpsIdx:{divIdx:id}}` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered record on load. Writes ONLY `cmd.divisions` + capital (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). NO RNG. `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand` (Inferred + 2 sources: Glatthaar, Weigley).

P. Hill / Hood / Pickett) while the rating mechanism is genuinely side-neutral and the sibling corps tier named both sides вҖ” the exact Lost-Cause over-celebration pattern CLAUDE.md #4 guards against. FIXED copy-only (byte-identical): added the Union counterpart (Hancock's II Corps divisions, Gibbon/Barlow) to the `divFoot` UI string + the `divisionCommand` `_note`. ## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-23 **Q11: THE COMMISSION MOVE вҖ” bring the documented POLITICAL GENERALS (Banks В· Butler В· Sigel В· McClernand В· Floyd В· Pillow) into your officer pool for political capital; rank and constituency are not competence** (overnight run, D109)

> **The GM "Commission" move is shipped** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.2/В§12.3 вҖ” "bring a new officer into the pool"). Beyond the generals the war hands you, the President now COMMISSIONS the documented POLITICAL GENERALS вҖ” **US Banks В· Butler В· Sigel В· McClernand**, **CS Floyd В· Pillow** вҖ” into his officer pool for **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the existing GM currency; no new resource, В§12), after which they are appointable / promotable / seatable like any general. A new President's-Desk **"Commission an officer вҖ” the political generals"** section lists each with his **LOW** combat OVR beside his **HIGH** political value, his constituency, an honest one-line record, and a Commission control (gated on capital + the `maxCommissions` 3-slate). It fills the GM layer's central TEACHING keystone вҖ” В§12.3's command-politics bind: these men were cheap to commission and weak in the field (Lincoln/Davis kept them for the factions, votes, and immigrant regiments they delivered, not their generalship), so once you appoint or seat one his low OVR drags the army's leadership (a commissioned Banks fields commandLeadership **49** vs Grant's **87**).
>
> **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose Commission (option C) over the symmetric AI-GM (B, [hard]) and a DIVISION sub-tier (lower-risk but thinner) because it fills the missing teaching keystone (the political-general bind the В§12.3 anti-gamey constraints are built around), reuses the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdPromote` byte-identical-until-used spine + the В§8 person concept, and adds 6 new citation-grade figures. ## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-23 **Q10: THE CORPS DEPTH-CHART вҖ” seat your generals into corps command over the Order-of-Battle tree; who you place (and whether his rank fits the billet) shapes how well the whole army fights** (overnight run, D108)

> **The GM depth-chart MOVE is shipped, built on the D106 OOB tree** (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.1/В§12.2/В§12.4 вҖ” "an army version of waiver/trading/transfer"). Beyond appointing the ARMY commander (the existing `cmdAppoint` billet), a new President's-Desk **"The Corps Command вҖ” Depth Chart"** section lets the President SEAT pool generals into the army's CORPS billets (IвҖ“IV Corps), spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` вҖ” the existing GM currency, no new resource). Each billet shows its seated commander (name + grade + OVR + a below-grade tell) with a Vacate control, or "Vacant" + a pool `<select>` + a Seat control (gated on capital); a live read-out shows the net leadership the staffed corps add. Teaches real command organization вҖ” Lee's First (Longstreet) and Second (Jackson) Corps vs the Army of the Potomac's churning corps commands; the rout of Howard's XI Corps at Chancellorsville.
>
> **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose the depth-chart MOVES (option A) over the symmetric AI-GM (option B, flagged [hard]) because A extends the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote` spine over the D106 substrate and is byte-identical-until-moved like Q9; the new officer-slot/vacancy concept the derived T15 corps lacked is the `cmd.corps` slot map + a side-aware grade-fit.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated corps commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership(C)` вҖ” an INPUT the bridge already reads вҖ” via `_cmdCorpsLift(C)` = `clamp( SUM over seated slots of (effectiveCorpsRating вҲ’ 64) Г— perSlotWeight, ВұliftCap )` (0.05 / cap 4). `effectiveCorpsRating` = the general's GM OVR (carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (6) when his CURRENT grade is below the **SIDE-AWARE** preferred grade. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership вҶ’ bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe, NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`). The army commander still weighs most (~Вұ17); the corps lift (Вұ4) is a secondary modifier (В§27).
>
> **THE SIDE-AWARE GRADE-FIT (historically precise; the Q9 synergy):** a US corps was a **Maj. Gen.'s** command, a CS corps a **Lt. Gen.'s** (the CS authorized the Lt. Gen. grade Sept. 18, 1862, promoting Longstreet/Jackson that Oct. to command the ANV's new corps). So on the shipped roster only CS **Stuart** (a Maj. Gen.) seats below grade over a corps; promoting him to Lt. Gen. (Q9) removes the penalty. `data/ratings.json` `corpsCommand`: `slots 4 В· seatCost 3 В· preferredGrade {US:"Maj. Gen.",CS:"Lt. Gen."} В· perSlotWeight 0.05 В· liftCap 4 В· belowGradePenalty 6 В· Inferred В· 2 sources`.
>

The army commander can't double-hold (excluded from the pool; `cmdAppoint` clears his corps). The seated commanders also NAME the player's DERIVED corps on the OOB board (pure display вҖ” the predicted edge is UNCHANGED; the enemy is never named; a "Garrison" node is never named).
>

Gen. grade date ("created Oct 1862") вҶ’ corrected to the Sept. 18, 1862 authorization + the Oct. promotions + the Nov. 6 reorganization.

## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-23 **Q8b: THE CAVALRY RECONNAISSANCE вҖ” "scout the enemy" tier-reveals the enemy Order of Battle, scaled by your appointed general's cavalry** (overnight run, D107)

> **The camp loop's deferred SCOUTING (В§15) is shipped, built on the D106 OOB board.** An **"Order a reconnaissance"** control inside the Command-desk Order-of-Battle board lets the President spend a small amount of **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` вҖ” the existing GM currency, also spent by appoint/promote; no new resource) to reveal the **enemy** order of battle to a TIER scaled by the appointed army commander's persona **`cavalry`** attribute. **Three tiers (В§15):** **light** (unscouted вҖ” the passive D106 estimate: force grade band + rough count + the CTA) вҶ’ **better** (scouted, cavalry < 65: the enemy commander NAMED + per-corps grade + a posture/terrain advisory, no per-brigade detail) вҶ’ **full** (scouted, cavalry вүҘ 65: the complete enemy OOB). With the 9 generals' cavalry, Grant (66) + Lee (70) вҶ’ full, the rest вҶ’ better; a no-appointee campaign uses the HISTORICAL DEFAULT commander's cavalry. Intel is **fresh per engagement** (the scout record is keyed to the next-battle id вҶ’ reverts to light when the battle changes). Teaches cavalry-as-the-army's-eyes вҖ” Stuart's rides, and the Gettysburg intelligence vacuum when his cavalry was absent (a real Confederate command failure, not glorified).

The corps-billet MOVES need a new officer-slot concept the derived T15 tree lacks вҖ” deferred next.

## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-22 **THE OOB-MAPPING SUBSTRATE вҖ” the strategic next-battle now maps to a structured Order of Battle; a read-only roster board ships on the Command desk** (overnight run, D106)

>
> **TWO SOURCES, ONE SHAPE (`fldOOBForSide`/`fldCampaignOOB`/`fldCampaignOOBHtml`):** a battle WITH a hand-built scenario (`fldScenarioData`) вҶ’ its REAL brigade OOB (real commanders + the authored provenance read via `_fldOOBProvFromNote`, reusing the Q7 reader `_fldOOBUnits`); a procedural battle вҶ’ a DETERMINISTIC corps/brigade tree split from `bd.us`/`bd.cs`/year, seeded by id+side (NO RNG). Derived billets are FORMATION-LABELED (I Corps В· 1st Brigade В· Garrison) with `commander:null` вҖ” **NEVER a fabricated officer** (CLAUDE.md #4/D92). The army-commander headline names only the player's APPOINTED general (+ his `_cmdGenRating` OVR) or the historical `cmd<Side>` (Verified). **ENEMY-FUZZY (В§15):** the board shows the PLAYER exact + the ENEMY fuzzy (grade + count + commander, no per-brigade detail) вҖ” the hook Q8b scouting DEEPENS via a higher `reveal` tier; the substrate returns FULL data for both sides for the GM/scouting to query.

## вҡЎ EARLIER вҖ” 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM Q9 вҖ” the GM PROMOTION economy (the first depth-chart MOVE: promote В· multi-currency В· merit gate)** (overnight run, D102)

> **The first real GM *move* beyond appoint/relieve is shipped.** On the President's-Desk Command tab there is now an **"Officer Corps вҖ” Promotions"** section: the President promotes a general one grade up a clean strategic ladder (**Brig. Gen. вҶ’ Maj. Gen. вҶ’ Lt. Gen. вҶ’ General**), spending a **multi-currency** budget вҖ” **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the primary, shared with relief/appointment) **+ a NEW seniority pool** (`cmd.seniority`, accrues over the campaign, capped) вҖ” and **merit-gated** by reputation. PURE INPUT-SEEDING + display, **byte-identical until the player promotes** (sandbox + all 9 battles proven byte-for-byte identical to committed HEAD `fc1d251`). Built on the existing `cmdAppoint`/`_cmdReliefCost` spine + the R-5 `fldPromotePerson` latent-command concept; entirely in `src/35-command.js` (the "Q9 (D102)" block) + a `promotion` config in `data/ratings.json`.
>
> **THE MERIT GATE (the honest history, the keystone):** each target grade carries a reputation **meritBar**. EARNED (rep вүҘ bar) вҶ’ a confidence bump (+3 rep); ABOVE merit (rep < bar) вҶ’ a Г—1.8 capital surcharge **+ a jealousy reputation HIT (вҲ’4)**. Because OVR = 0.55В·skill + 0.45В·reputation, **over-promoting a favorite past his record can LOWER his OVR** вҖ” rank without merit doesn't make a good commander (teaches the real command politics Lincoln navigated; anti-Lost-Cause: merit, not grade, is competence). Leapfrogging a passed-over senior adds a seniority surcharge.
>
> **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path, no fudge):** a promotion lifts the general's effective skill by a small **BOUNDED** amount вҖ” `_cmdPromoteSkillLift` = (rankBase grade-delta Г— 0.92), clamped to **вүӨ6** вҖ” added inside the EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen, C)`, which flows ONLY through the existing `_cmdGenRating вҶ’ commandLeadership вҶ’` the bridge LEADERSHIP facet (an INPUT the sim already reads; `commandMarginEdge` reads aggression/caution, untouched). `cmdPromote` writes ONLY `clk.capital`/`cmd.seniority`/`cmd.promotions`/`cmd.reputation` вҖ” **never the scoreboard** (D74/D94 wall). **0 lift when un-promoted вҶ’ every pre-Q9 reading byte-identical** (live-sanity proven: a promotion stores "Lt. Gen.", lifts commandLeadership 79вҶ’80; the un-promoted skill reads identical with/without C for all 20 generals).
>
> **New fns (`src/35-command.js`):** `_cmdPromoCfg`/`_cmdRankBase`/`_cmdBaseGrade`/`_cmdGradeIdx`/`_cmdNextGrade`/`_cmdCurrentGrade`/`_cmdPromoteSkillLift`/`_cmdLeapfrogged`/`_cmdPromoteInfo`/`cmdPromote`/`_cmdPromoRow`/`_cmdPromotionsHTML`/`_cmdNum`; EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen,C)` (+lift), `cmdInit` (seeds + load-clamps `seniority`, seeds `promotions`), `cmdOnResolve` (accrues `seniority` вҖ” invisible/byte-identical), `cmdRenderTab` (+section), `cmdWireTab` (+promote buttons); call sites `_cmdGenRating`/`cmdActiveTraits`/`_cmdActiveCard` now thread C. **Data:** the `promotion` block in `data/ratings.json` (ladder В· meritBar В· capitalCost В· aboveMeritMul В· seniority{CostBase,Leapfrog,Start,PerTurn,WinBonus,Cap} В· earnedRepBonus В· aboveMeritRepHit В· skillLiftWeight В· skillLiftCap В· topCommandPreferredGrade).

## вҡЎ CONTINUE HERE вҖ” 2026-06-22 **RATING SYSTEM R-4 вҖ” the X-FACTORS (the dramatic "in the zone" surge, inside the no-fudge wall)** (overnight run, D98)

> **The Madden layer now SWINGS a fight вҖ” provably without ever touching the scoreboard.** An X-Factor badge enters "in the zone" when its situational trigger fires and surges on ONE channel, hard-capped. Demonstrated: a single `foot_cavalry` badge on one CS sandbox brigade **flipped a deterministic US win into a CS win** (same seed), yet the total-casualty shift was only **17.2%** and the command aura peaked at **0.47 < the 0.9 wall** вҖ” the rating reaches the result EMERGENTLY through bounded inputs, never by writing `cas`/`victory`/`men`/`sev`.
>
> **`fldXFactorStep(dt)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** gated on `__FIELD.badges`; for each unit carrying an `rung:"xfactor"` badge (`_fldUnitXFactors`), `_fldXFactorInZone` tests activation (march_vigor=moving В· his_offensive=moving/charging В· ammo_low_defend=ammo<12 & not charging В· last_stand_defend=holding & (low morale or a friendly routing within 220yd) В· usct_assault/mass_assault=charging В· flanking=cav & charging). In the zone it surges **ONE channel = the declared lever**: a NON-speed X-Factor sets `u._xfActive = fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"xfactor")` (arcade 1.45 / balanced 1.20 / historian 1.08); a SPEED X-Factor (Foot Cavalry / The Slows) sets `u._spdMul` only (capped [0.85,1.15]) and does NOT also surge the aura. One-shot вҡЎ `fldAnnounce`+`fldScenarioBanner` (`_xfOn` rising edge); `_xfGlow` marker pulse; deterministic `_fldXfDecay`вҶ’1 out of zone. **NO RNG.** A unit with no X-Factor is wholly untouched вҶ’ byte-identical.
>
> **`fldXFactorApplyCmd(u)`:** `u.cmdBonus = min(FLDO.CMD_BONUS_CAP, (cmdBonus||0)*_xfActive)` вҖ” pushes the summed aura toward the **0.9 wall, never beyond**; strict no-op unless active. Called in `fldSimStep` AFTER `fldOfficersStep` (aura summed first), gated on `badges` (NOT officers) so both surge channels share one gate.
>

## вҡЎ CONTINUE HERE вҖ” 2026-06-21 **CHICKAMAUGA вҖ” the 3-phase Western epic shipped + adversarially hardened** (the woods вҶ’ Longstreet's breakthrough вҶ’ Thomas at Snodgrass Hill; probe 18/18) вҖ” D90

> **Chickamauga is playable and verified вҖ” the bloodiest battle of the Western theater, the fourth multi-phase epic, built on the T8 engine.** A new **вҡ” BATTLE вҖ” CHICKAMAUGA (1863)** main-menu button (rank 60, after Vicksburg) opens the side-choice card; command Bragg/Longstreet's army or Thomas's defense across three sectors in sequence: **P0 The Battle in the Woods (Sep 19)** вҖ” a confused meeting engagement in blind timber; the Union line holds the road (historical). **P1 Longstreet's Breakthrough (Sep 20)** вҖ” the Wood gap order pulls a US division out of line at the moment Longstreet's column strikes the Brotherton farm; the CS pours through and routs the right (the decisive **scoreWeight-3** phase). **P2 The Rock of Chickamauga** вҖ” Thomas holds Snodgrass Hill / Horseshoe Ridge until dusk, reinforced by Granger/Steedman, saving the army. Anti-Lost-Cause: **contingency over genius** (a staff blunder + a timing coincidence, not martial superiority) and **the squandered victory** (Bragg fails to pursue вҶ’ the siege of Chattanooga вҶ’ the November reversal).
>
> **Framing (decide-&-log, no fork):** the C2 "Chickamauga/Chattanooga" item = a matched PAIR of separate 3-phase epics (the Antietam/Gettysburg precedent), each its own milestone. **Top-level `attacker: CS` / `defender: US` across all 3 phases** (the Army of the Cumberland fought on the defensive) вҖ” the CS player is the offensive, the US player holds. This sets **Chattanooga up as the US-offensive MIRROR** (the next milestone; design brief at `.tmp/chattanooga-design.md`, which also banks the engine-grain lessons from this build). Universal gun model only; **no per-battle damage fudge** (D74).

> **Balance (AI-vs-AI, 32 seeds, deterministic):** P0 US-holds 32/32 (mutual bloodbath ~2,400 each); P1 **CS breakthrough 32/32** (US routed cheaply, US:CS ~5.1); P2 **US-holds 32/32**, CS attacker pays **CS:US ~3.0** (the Fredericksburg failed-assault lesson); **aggregate CS 32/32** (CS 3 / US 2). A human US player who closes the Wood gap in P1 **overturns** the battle (the alt-history hinge). The CS won the field yet **bled MORE in aggregate** (~70k vs ~63k / 8 seeds) вҖ” the costly-victory teaching, probe-guarded.

## вҡЎ CONTINUE HERE вҖ” 2026-06-21 **ENGINEERING CORPS вҖ” increment 3: PONTOON BRIDGING shipped + hardened вҶ’ THE CORPS IS COMPLETE** (the pontoon train; player-only/byte-identical; probe 22/22) вҖ” D89

> **The Tactical Engineering Corps is DONE вҖ” all 3 of Aaron's locked "all of the above" (entrench + abatis + pontoons).** A NEW **opt-in river** (`__FIELD.terrain.rivers[]`) actually gates movement: a river is impassable except at a **crossing** вҖ” a **shallow ford** (passable, slow + fatiguing), a **deep ford** (fordable only at Arcade; needs a bridge at Balanced/Historian), or a player-laid **pontoon bridge** (key **N** / "Pontoon" button): an infantry pioneer detail on the near bank lays a bridge over realism-scaled time, opening a fast crossing. Surfaced via the **Skirmish вҶ’ Ground вҶ’ "River crossing"** option (+ an `opts.river` sandbox flag for the probe). The **B-5 realism slider** scales sapper speed, ford slow, AND fordable-vs-requires-pontoon; the strategic **Engineer Works Corps** (`bridgeArmy.engineering`) lays bridges faster on a campaign launch (the A1 anchor, via `__FIELD.engCorpsSpeed`). 2D slate-water band + boat-deck pontoons + ford stepping-stones + labels (CVD-safe, reduceMotion-safe); 3D water plane + pontoon boats/deck; a citation-grade Fredericksburg/Rappahannock + James-River-1864 teaching card.
>
> **Architecture (byte-identical):** the active gate REUSES the two T0 seams reserved for it вҖ” `fldEngMoveFactor` (ford slow) + `fldEngMoveGate` (returns a clamped bank point for an illegal water step). New T13 fns: `fldEngInstallRiver`, `fldEngCrossAt`, `_fldRiverNearest/_fldRiverBankPoint/_fldEngBridgeSite`, `fldSelPontoon`, the pontoon loop in `fldEngStep`, `fldEngDrawWater2d`, `fld3dBuildWater` + pontoon sync in `fld3dSyncEng`. **No shipped scenario declares `terrain.rivers` and the AI never lays a pontoon** вҶ’ every AI-vs-AI baseline byte-for-byte unchanged (every read gated by `rv && rv.length` / `engPontoons`; reset per-launch + per-phase). One T0 seam edit: `fldStepMovement` now settles a no-progress river clamp to HOLD (the bug-hunt's soft-deadlock fix) вҖ” `eg`-gated, so riverless baselines are identical.
>
> **DECISIONS (decide-&-log, no fork surfaced):** Bull Run's creek/Stone Bridge stay COSMETIC (making them live would regress a shipped, probed battle + break byte-identity); the active river is the opt-in feature, and the teaching card cites the Rappahannock as the historical anchor. AI river-pathing / AI-built works is the named T13 extension point (player-tool this increment, like D87/D88), so a river skirmish frames the PLAYER as the attacker forcing the crossing (river installed between the player's home edge and the objective, either side) while the AI defends the far bank.
>
> **Bug-hunt (19 agents, Opus): 8 confirmed + 6 critic, all fixed.** HIGH: the gate's origin test let a unit on an open ford **sidestep into deep water and wade the band** вҶ’ block entering blocked water from anywhere except already-blocked water + a midpoint sample (tangential bends). HIGH: the **3D water plane was buried under the opaque terrain** вҶ’ raised to a thin on-ground sheet (+ fords lifted, no z-fight). HIGH: a unit ordered across impassable water **marched in place forever, fatigueвҶ’100** вҶ’ settle to HOLD at the bank. HIGH: the river skirmish was degenerate for a CS player вҶ’ river placed by player side. MED: silent crossing refusal вҶ’ aria-live halt announce + HUD line. LOW: dupe-span message; pontoon `side` + per-side cap.
>
> **Verification:** build GATE OK; `probe-engineering-corps` **22/22**, 0 pe; full no-regression **GREEN (21 probes byte-identical: field 13 В· bullrun 15 В· shiloh 29 В· malvern 24 В· antietam 16 В· fredericksburg 22 В· chancellorsville 24 В· gettysburg 16 В· vicksburg 18 В· roster 8 В· visuals ok [texWarn 0] В· custom 9 В· fog 13 В· ai 15 В· autopause 13 В· campaign-link 16 В· officers 15 В· logistics 14 В· arms 23 В· presets 26 В· csplayer 16; diag-classic `nonBlank:346`; boot/t1 ok; 0 pageerrors)**; WCAG-AA on all new UI (вүҘ4.5:1, CVD-safe). Also added the long-missing B/X/N engineering keys to the help overlay.

## вҡЎ CONTINUE HERE вҖ” 2026-06-18 Custom Battle Builder C4 complete вң… вҖ” single-phase authoring, import/export, slots, launch gate green

> **Custom Battle Builder C4 is built and verified.** New `src/tactical/T11-custom-battle.js` adds a first-class main-menu builder flow for player-authored real-time tactical scenarios. It covers scenario name/date/place, sides/briefs, objective, field size, terrain hills/woods/walls/markers, OOB units, artillery/gun counts, reinforcement/deployment timing, optional leaders, supply trains, teaching cards, provenance, JSON import/export, shareable JSON, and six local persistence slots.
>
> **Architecture decision:** C4 is intentionally **single-phase V1**. Phase authoring remains deferred until a UI for `phases[]` can be proven as safe as authored historical phase data. Custom scenarios do **not** enter `fldScenarioRegistry()`; `fldScenarioData(id)` only falls back to `fldCustomScenarioData(id)` for explicit `custom_...` IDs. That preserves the exact historical battle roster while still launching valid custom scenarios through the same single-phase `fldScenarioInit` data path. Field size is reset every launch via `FLD.BASE_FIELD_W/H`, then a scenario may apply `field.w/h` safely.
>
> **Validation guardrails:** required metadata, safe unique IDs, malformed/unsafe JSON keys, duplicate IDs, bounds and numeric clamps, objective placement, reinforcement timing, side ownership, leader attach ownership, realistic artillery crew counts (12-40 per gun), forbidden combat/damage keys, and `phases[]` are all blocked. Custom artillery uses the universal `guns` model only; no per-custom-battle damage fudge was added.
>
> **Focused probe:** `tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` verifies builder render, validation failures, valid scenario creation, export/import round trip, UI malformed-import rejection, slot save/list/load/delete, explicit custom-ID launch contract, universal gun model, field-size reset, no phase leak, no Classic `G.battle`, and no historical registry contamination. Current result: **9/9 steps ok, 0 fail**, with `tools/shots/probe-custom-battle-builder.json/png`.
>
> **Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` вҶ’ GATE OK; `node tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` вҶ’ 9/9; `node tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` вҶ’ 8/8; `node tools/probe-field.mjs` вҶ’ 13/13; `node tools/probe-bullrun.mjs` вҶ’ 15/15; `node tools/probe-malvern-hill.mjs` вҶ’ 24/24; `node tools/probe-antietam.mjs` вҶ’ 16/16; `node tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` вҶ’ 22/22; `node tools/probe-chancellorsville.mjs` вҶ’ 24/24; `node tools/probe-gettysburg.mjs` вҶ’ 16/16; `node tools/probe-shiloh.mjs` вҶ’ 29/29; `node tools/probe-officers.mjs` вҶ’ 15/15; `node tools/probe-logistics.mjs` вҶ’ 14/14; `node tools/probe-arms.mjs` вҶ’ 23/23; `node tools/probe-presets.mjs` вҶ’ 26/26; `node tools/probe-csplayer.mjs` вҶ’ 16/16; `node tools/probe-campaign-link.mjs` вҶ’ 16/16; `node tools/probe-tactical-visuals.mjs` вҶ’ 6/6; `node tools/bootprobe.mjs` вҶ’ ok=true with known/tolerated 404 resource console entries; `node tools/t1probe.mjs` вҶ’ ok=true; `node tools/diag-classic.mjs` вҶ’ Classic paints, nonBlank 346; `git diff --check` вҶ’ clean.

## 1 В· THE PROJECT IN ONE PARAGRAPH
"The Civil War" is becoming **the definitive teaching wargame: Ultimate General: Gettysburg's combat FEEL + Paradox-grade strategic DEPTH + a museum's historical RIGOR** вҖ” all three, no compromise. You are the **President (Lincoln or Davis)** running the entire war (economy, politics, diplomacy, morale, generals, the home front) AND commanding the battles in a real-time, gridless, drag-to-maneuver tactical engine вҖ” wrapped in a PhD-level history + alternate-history teaching layer where scholarly consensus is the *favored-but-not-guaranteed* path. **The governing design law (Aaron's central tension, resolved): the simple low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun CORE that stands alone; ALL depth is optional вҖ” auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able; education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real in-game mastery (so learning and fun pull the SAME direction).** One engine must serve the pure-battle player, the grand-strategist, and the PhD-historian simultaneously.

## 2 В· WHERE THINGS STAND (run h, verified)
- **Classic (hex, turn-based) is FROZEN/finished** вҖ” the complete hex lineage + its 3D-skin "Modern." NEVER regress it (`tools/diag-classic.mjs` every splice).
- **Shipped + GPU-verified this run (all reusable):** procedural unit motion; **131 real PD-photo leader portraits** (`assets/portraits/`, license-gated, side-split for Anderson/Gregg) with a closure refactor + upgraded engraving fallback; a fuller period UI pass (drawn order-icons, engraved frames, brass portrait mat). Plus the inherited cinematic 3D foundation (PBR terrain, HDRI, ACES/bloom post-FX, weather, props, camera) and the adaptive period audio score.
- **The shipped "Modern" is only a 3D re-skin of the hex-turn engine** вҖ” it does NOT play like UG:G. The real-time tactical engine + the grand-strategy owner-mode are **NOT built yet** вҖ” that's the next work.
- **DESIGN: 63 decisions LOCKED** across a 35-round popup design session (Aaron). Fully captured in `GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN.md` (Parts IвҖ“III). **No new-engine code written yet** вҖ” the next chat builds from the spec.

## 3 В· THE DOCS (read in this order вҖ” you have zero prior context)
1. **`GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN.md`** вҖ” THE DESIGN LAW. All 63 locked decisions: Part I (rounds 1вҖ“10: player/economy/executive/morale/alt-history/upgrades/education/victory/modes/first-build), Part II (rounds 11вҖ“20: diplomacy/slavery/politics/naval/map/generals/soldiers/intel/events/replay), Part III (rounds 21вҖ“33: **the depthвҶ”simplicity balance** + presentation), В§27 **the balance principle**, В§13/В§24/В§28 decision indexes.
2. **`HISTORICAL-DATA.md`** вҖ” citation-grade content (211KB, 18-agent research): First Bull Run full OOB (Union + CSA), weapons/ballistics with ranges, USCT (structure/battles/criticism), the historiography framework, PD image sources. Feeds OOBs, weapon stats, debate cards, the codex.
3. **`MODERN-UGG-PLAN.md`** вҖ” the real-time tactical battle engine spec (built SECOND, after the strategic layer).
4. **`RUN-LOG.md` В§"run h"** вҖ” what shipped + the pivot + this design session; skim В§"run g"/В§"run f" for the 3D foundation.
5. **`REVIEW-QUEUE.md` top** + **`GRAPHICS-RUN-CONTINUE.md` В§TOOLCHAIN/GOTCHAS** вҖ” the splice/gate/real-GPU-shot toolchain + the bare-name-globals / async-THREE / override-by-redeclaration lessons.

## 4 В· ARCHITECTURE DECISION (run h вҖ” important)
**Modularize via a zero-dependency build step.** The scope (50вҖ“100k+ lines) outgrows the single 14k-line file. Author the new engine in **source modules**; a tiny **node concat script** assembles the one shippable `civil_war_generals.html` (keep the $0/portable/open-and-play deliverable + `play.command`). Set this up FIRST in S0. Classic + the existing engine stay intact through the transition (move them into the build later, carefully, or keep the current HTML as the base the build appends to). Gate the BUILT output (parse/hex/Classic-regression). This replaces the append-only-single-file splice model for new work вҖ” but the gate discipline carries over.

## 5 В· BUILD ORDER & PHASES (Aaron: STRATEGIC-FIRST, confirmed twice)
**Phase group S (grand-strategy owner-mode) FIRST, then phase group P (real-time tactical).** Battles use the EXISTING engine via a clean bridge until the UG:G engine swaps in.
- **S0 вҖ” scaffold:** set up the module/build system; expand the War Department (`G.campaign.{clock,muster,warroom}`) into the President's-desk shell (period war-room UI); strategic-turn loop; save. Layered scenario onboarding (start ~1861, limited toolset).
- **S1 вҖ” economy** (full asymmetric model + finance/inflation/blockade).
- **S2 вҖ” executive decisions + 3-layer morale + the 1864 election; the advisor/cabinet system** (the linchpin: auto-manage + recommend + TEACH, per-domain delegation).
- **S3 вҖ” alt-history engine** (tiered divergence + hinge-points + emergent toggle + curated scenarios; deterministic-by-performance with consensus framing; the "your war vs history" tracker).
- **S4 вҖ” education layer** (multi-voice debate cards + deep-dives + codex from HISTORICAL-DATA.md; ambient teaching; difficulty/realism sliders; play-style presets; full a11y).
- **S5 вҖ” victory/defeat** (asymmetric paths incl. **negotiated peace for both sides**, military-only hard-loss) + all campaign scopes; wire existing battles through the bridge вҶ’ **playable full owner-mode war.**
- **THEN P0вҖ“P5** (`MODERN-UGG-PLAN.md`): the real-time UG:G tactical engine (First Bull Run vertical slice first), swapping in behind the bridge.
Each phase: gate + real-GPU self-verify (probes you READ) + Classic no-regression + left in a working, polished state (ship-quality iteratively).

## 6 В· THE BALANCE PRINCIPLE (design law вҖ” apply to EVERY system)
The simple, low-micro UG:G battle is the always-fun core that works on its own. Every deep system is optional вҖ” auto-managed by characterful advisors, delegable per-domain, preset-gated, fluidly dial-able mid-campaign. Education is ambient, never blocks play, and confers real mastery (learning is rewarded by winning, not a chore-score). Presets + sliders let each player set their own balance. **If a feature forces depth on a battle-first player, it's wrong; if it denies depth to a strategist/historian, it's wrong.** (Full statement: GRAND-STRATEGY-PLAN В§27.)

## 7 В· TOOLCHAIN, GATES, GOTCHAS (proven вҖ” reuse)
- **Gates every change:** `.bak` вҶ’ parse (`node --check` the built/extracted `<script>`) вҶ’ invalid-hex grep `0x[0-9a-fA-F]*[g-z]` = 0 вҶ’ collision-grep new fns = 0. With the new build step, gate the assembled output.
- **Real-GPU self-verify (READ the PNGs/probes):** `tools/shot-postfx.mjs`, `tools/shot-gpu.mjs`, `tools/shot-ui.mjs`, `tools/probe-motion.mjs`, `tools/probe-portraits.mjs`, `tools/bootprobe.mjs`, `tools/diag-classic.mjs`. Real GPU = **Intel UHD 617** via headed Chrome `--use-angle=metal`. A real-time sim/strategic loop needs an EMPIRICAL probe (sample state over frames), not just screenshots. Stale server: `lsof -ti tcp:8765 | xargs kill`.
- **Perf target:** smooth on the Intel UHD 617 at Auto tier; instancing/LOD/perf-tiers mandatory.
- **CRITICAL gotchas:** `G`/`HEX`/`PALETTE`/`THREE_BASE` are bare-name lexical globals (never `window.G`); THREE loads async (no top-level `new THREE.*`); override-by-redeclaration (last def wins); never a literal `*/` in a block comment; honor `reduceMotion` + `gfxQuality`; **NEVER regress Classic**; $0/free-CC0; Verified/Inferred provenance on all history.
- **Asset pipeline (historical run-H note; current top block supersedes live setup):** PD images via the run-h portrait pattern (Wikipedia REST summary вҶ’ Commons license API PD-gate вҶ’ download вҶ’ `sips` resize). Extend to weapons/flags/USCT. Blender MCP remains available for future explicit 3D asset jobs (PolyHaven CC0 / Sketchfab), but Blender does not need to stay open unless a Phase-H asset task starts; free Hyper3D trial is drained.
